# Crono$Emojis



Devuelve el listado completos de Emojis reconocidos por el estándar UNICODE. 

Esta información está generada a partir del fichero [emoji-test.txt](https://unicode.org/Public/emoji/13.0/emoji-test.txt) proporcionado por Unicode Consortium.


<div class="mt-1 mb-2 row">
  <div class="col-lg-12">

``` sql
select 
	GroupName,
	SubgroupName,
	Name,
	Emoji
from Crono$Emojis
where SubgroupName='face-smiling'
order by emoji
```

  <b-button class="float-right btn" size="sm" v-b-modal.modal-1 style="background-color: #3eaf7c">Ver SQL compilado</b-button>

  <b-modal id="modal-1" size="lg" title="Ver SQL compilado" :hide-footer="true" > 
``` sql
SELECT
  GroupName,
  SubgroupName,
  Name,
  Emoji
FROM
  (SELECT
     GroupName,
     SubgroupName,
     Name,
     concat(CASE WHEN c1>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c1/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c1%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c1) END,CASE WHEN c2>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c2/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c2%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c2) END,CASE WHEN c3>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c3/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c3%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c3) END,CASE WHEN c4>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c4/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c4%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c4) END,CASE WHEN c5>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c5/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c5%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c5) END,CASE WHEN c6>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c6/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c6%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c6) END,CASE WHEN c7>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c7/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c7%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c7) END,CASE WHEN c8>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c8/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c8%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c8) END) AS Emoji,
     CASE WHEN c1>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c1/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c1%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c1) END AS Char1,
     CASE WHEN c2>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c2/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c2%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c2) END AS Char2,
     CASE WHEN c3>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c3/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c3%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c3) END AS Char3,
     CASE WHEN c4>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c4/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c4%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c4) END AS Char4,
     CASE WHEN c5>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c5/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c5%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c5) END AS Char5,
     CASE WHEN c6>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c6/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c6%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c6) END AS Char6,
     CASE WHEN c7>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c7/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c7%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c7) END AS Char7,
     CASE WHEN c8>65535 THEN nchar(CAST(0xD7C0+(c8/1024) AS int))+nchar(CAST(0xDC00+(c8%1024) AS int)) ELSE nchar(c8) END AS Char8
   FROM (
     SELECT 'Smileys & Emotion' GroupName,'face-smiling' SubGroupName,'grinning face' Name,0x1F600 c1,NULL c2,NULL c3,NULL c4,NULL c5,NULL c6,NULL c7,NULL c8
```
